# <a name="obsolete-members-in-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="bbb2a-105">Устаревшие члены в .NET Framework</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bbb2a-105">Obsolete members in .NET Framework</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bbb2a-106">В этой статье перечислены члены типов, устаревшие в .NET Framework 4.5 и выше.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bbb2a-106">This article list the type members that are obsolete in .NET Framework 4.5 and later versions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bbb2a-107">Члены типа группируются по сборкам.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bbb2a-107">Type members are grouped by assembly.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bbb2a-108">В этой статье не перечисляются члены устаревших типов.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bbb2a-108">This article doesn't list the members of obsolete types.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bbb2a-109">См. [список устаревших типов](obsolete-types.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bbb2a-109">For a list of obsolete types, see [Obsolete types](obsolete-types.md).</span></span>

## <a name="iehostdll-and-ieexecexe"></a><span data-ttu-id="bbb2a-1111">IEHost.dll and IEExec.exe</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bbb2a-1111">IEHost.dll and IEExec.exe</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bbb2a-1112">Сборки IEHost.dll и IEExec.exe удалены из .NET Framework.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bbb2a-1112">The IEHost.dll and IEExec.exe assemblies have been removed from .NET Framework.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bbb2a-1113">Все их типы и члены устарели и не поддерживаются, начиная с .NET Framework 4.5.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bbb2a-1113">All of their types and their members are obsolete and are not supported in .NET Framework 4.5 and later.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bbb2a-1114">Эти сборки использовались для размещения элементов управления Windows Forms и для запуска исполняемых файлов в Internet Explorer.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bbb2a-1114">These assemblies were used to host Windows Forms controls and to run executables in Internet Explorer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bbb2a-1115">Взамен этой технологии рекомендуется использовать ClickOnce, XAML-приложения браузера (XBAP) и Microsoft Silverlight.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bbb2a-1115">Alternatives to this technology include ClickOnce, XAML Browser Applications (XBAP), and Microsoft Silverlight.</span></span>

> |<xref:Microsoft.VisualBasic.MyServices.RegistryProxy?displayProperty=nameWithType>|<xref:Microsoft.VisualBasic.MyServices.RegistryProxy.DynData%2A>|<span data-ttu-id="bbb2a-1184">Раздел реестра `DynData` применим только на платформе Win9x, для которой эта версия .NET Framework не предназначена.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bbb2a-1184">The `DynData` registry key works only on Win9x, which isn't supported by this version of the .NET Framework.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bbb2a-1185">Вместо этого используйте раздел реестра `PerformanceData`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bbb2a-1185">Use the `PerformanceData` registry key instead.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bbb2a-1186">В одной из будущих версий платформы это свойство будет удалено.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bbb2a-1186">This property will be removed from a future version of the Framework.</span></span>|
